+        thread_ts = q["slack_thread_ts"]
+        oldest = q["slack_last_reply_ts"]
+        # Per-thread channel (v10). NULL on legacy rows posted before the
+        # status-reports split — fall back to SLACK_CHANNEL_ID for those.
+        channel_id = q.get("slack_channel_id") or SLACK_CHANNEL_ID
+        if not channel_id:
+            continue
+        try:
+            replies = fetch_thread_replies(
+                SLACK_BOT_TOKEN, channel_id, thread_ts, oldest=oldest
+            )
+        except SlackAPIError as exc:
+            logger.error(
+                f"Reply fetch failed for {q['ticker']}@{q['event_date']}: {exc}"
+            )
+            continue
+        if not replies:
+            continue
+
+        kind = q["slack_question_kind"] or "xcheck"
+        ctx = ReplyContext(
+            ticker=q["ticker"],
+            event_date=q["event_date"],
+            kind=kind,
+            finnhub_date=q["event_date"] if kind == "xcheck" else None,
+            yf_dates=_yf_dates_from_signature(q["last_xcheck_yf_dates"]),
+        )
+
+        latest_ts = oldest
+        for reply in replies:
+            if reply.is_bot:
+                latest_ts = reply.ts
+                continue
+            action = parse_reply(reply.text, ctx)
+
+            # `acked` counts acks ACTUALLY posted (incremented next to each
+            # _ack_in_thread, only when not dry-run) so the summary matches
+            # reality rather than the parser's intent.
+            if action.action == ACT_HELP:
+                if not dry_run:
+                    _ack_in_thread(thread_ts, format_help(kind), channel_id)
+                    acked += 1
+            elif action.action == ACT_STATUS:
+                if not dry_run:
+                    _ack_in_thread(thread_ts, format_status(q, today), channel_id)
+                    acked += 1
+            elif action.action == ACT_UNKNOWN:
+                if not dry_run:
+                    _ack_in_thread(thread_ts, f":x: {action.error}", channel_id)
+                    acked += 1
+            else:
+                if not dry_run:
+                    override_ack = _apply_action(
+                        conn, q, action, today, cal_service=cal_service
+                    )
+                    # An override (e.g. a deferred lock) replaces the parser's
+                    # default success ack so we never tell the user a date is
+                    # pinned when it isn't — and it means the action did NOT
+                    # mutate state, so track it separately for the summary.
+                    if override_ack is not None:
+                        deferred += 1
+                    ack_text = override_ack if override_ack is not None else action.ack
+                    if ack_text:
+                        _ack_in_thread(thread_ts, ack_text, channel_id)
+                        acked += 1
+
+            latest_ts = reply.ts
+            processed += 1
+
+        if not dry_run and latest_ts and latest_ts != oldest:
+            advance_reply_watermark(conn, q["ticker"], q["event_date"], latest_ts)
+
+    logger.info(
+        f"--check-replies: {processed} reply(ies) processed, "
+        f"{acked} ack(s) posted ({deferred} deferred), "
+        f"{snoozed_reopened} snoozed reopened"
+    )
+    conn.close()
+
+
+# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
+# Date-lock management (D2)
+# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
+
+
+def _parse_lock_arg(value: str) -> tuple[str, str]:
+    """Parse a TICKER:YYYY-MM-DD argument. Raises ValueError on bad input."""
+    if ":" not in value:
+        raise ValueError(f"Expected TICKER:YYYY-MM-DD, got {value!r}")
+    ticker, event_date = value.split(":", 1)
+    ticker = ticker.strip().upper()
+    event_date = event_date.strip()
+    # Validate date
+    date.fromisoformat(event_date)
+    if not ticker:
+        raise ValueError("Ticker cannot be empty")
+    return ticker, event_date
+
+
+def run_set_lock(target: str, locked: bool):
+    """Set or clear the date-lock on an event. target format: TICKER:YYYY-MM-DD."""
+    try:
+        ticker, event_date = _parse_lock_arg(target)
+    except ValueError as exc:
+        logger.error(f"Invalid lock argument: {exc}")
+        sys.exit(1)
+
+    conn = init_db()
+    ok = set_date_lock(conn, ticker, event_date, locked)
+    conn.close()
+
+    if not ok:
+        logger.error(
+            f"No event found for {ticker} on {event_date}. "
+            f"Nothing to {'lock' if locked else 'unlock'}."
+        )
+        sys.exit(1)
+
+    verb = "Locked" if locked else "Unlocked"
+    logger.info(f"{verb} {ticker} {event_date}")
+
+
+def run_list_locks():
+    """Print currently-locked events."""
+    conn = init_db()
+    locks = list_locked_events(conn)
+    conn.close()
+
+    if not locks:
+        print("No events are currently date-locked.")
+        return
+    print(f"{len(locks)} event(s) currently date-locked:")
+    for lock in locks:
+        ticker = lock["ticker"]
+        ev_date = lock["event_date"]
+        hour = lock["event_hour"] or "TBD"
+        tier = lock["tier"]
+        co = f" — {lock['company_name']}" if lock["company_name"] else ""
+        print(f"  {ticker} (T{tier}) {ev_date} {hour}{co}")
+
+
+# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
+# CLI
+# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
+
+
+def main():
+    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(
+        description="Earnings Intelligence System — earnings calendar sync and workflow"
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--dry-run",
+        action="store_true",
+        help="Preview external writes (Calendar/TickTick/Slack) and skip the "
+             "reported flag. NOT fully side-effect-free: still upserts events + "
+             "estimate snapshots into SQLite.",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--populate-db-only",
+        action="store_true",
+        help="Alias for --dry-run, named for the CI use of seeding the SQLite "
+             "DB with events/estimates without any external writes.",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--backfill",
+        action="store_true",
+        help="Also check the past 30 days for any missed earnings",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--cleanup",
+        action="store_true",
+        help="Scan calendar for duplicate events and delete extras",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--no-ticktick",
+        action="store_true",
+        help="Skip TickTick task creation",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--ticktick-status",
+        action="store_true",
+        help="Show TickTick earnings review queue status",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--weekly-digest",
+        action="store_true",
+        help="Build and send the weekly earnings digest (Slack + email HTML for MCP draft)",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--check-results",
+        action="store_true",
+        help="Check for newly-reported earnings on --date (default: today); post results to Slack",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--check-missed-results",
+        action="store_true",
+        help="EDGAR backstop: alert when a Tier 1/2 name reported (SEC 8-K "
+             "Item 2.02) but Finnhub has no actuals yet (the FIVE-class miss)",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--date",
+        type=str,
+        default=None,
+        help="Target date (YYYY-MM-DD) for --check-results. Defaults to today.",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--no-heartbeat",
+        action="store_true",
+        help="Skip the Slack success heartbeat at the end of the run",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--reconcile-calendar",
+        action="store_true",
+        help="Detect and fix calendar/Finnhub date drift; silent no-op if in sync",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--lock",
+        metavar="TICKER:YYYY-MM-DD",
+        help="Lock an event's date so sync/reconcile won't overwrite it with Finnhub",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--unlock",
+        metavar="TICKER:YYYY-MM-DD",
+        help="Remove a date lock",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--list-locks",
+        action="store_true",
+        help="Show all currently date-locked events",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--cross-check",
+        action="store_true",
+        help="Compare Finnhub's upcoming Tier 1/2 dates against yfinance; alert on disagreement",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--refresh-descriptions",
+        action="store_true",
+        help="Rewrite title + description for all tagged upcoming calendar events from current DB state",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--check-announcements",
+        action="store_true",
+        help="Scan configured IR RSS feeds (ir_feeds.json) for earnings-date announcements; upgrade estimated Tier 1 events to confirmed when found",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--check-ir-emails",
+        action="store_true",
+        help="Scan Gmail (via gmail_token.json) for IR-alert emails on Tier 1/2 estimated events; upgrade to confirmed and store the Gmail thread URL",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--check-replies",
+        action="store_true",
+        help="Poll Slack threads for replies on open questions; apply commands (lock/wait/snooze/ignore/etc) to DB state",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--consensus-preview",
+        action="store_true",
+        help="Build the pre-earnings consensus-metrics preview (StreetAccount §9A) "
+             "for upcoming Tier-1 reporters and post to #street-account",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--preview-ticker",
+        type=str,
+        default=None,
+        metavar="TICKER",
+        help="Restrict --consensus-preview to a single ticker's next upcoming event (any tier)",
+    )
+    parser.add_argument(
+        "--preview-days",
+        type=int,
+        default=3,
+        help="Look-ahead window (days) for --consensus-preview reporter selection (default: 3)",
+    )
+    args = parser.parse_args()
+
+    # --populate-db-only is a self-documenting alias for --dry-run (DB writes
+    # only, no external side effects). Fold it in so all downstream checks of
+    # args.dry_run see it.
+    if getattr(args, "populate_db_only", False):
+        args.dry_run = True
+
+    if args.list_locks:
+        run_list_locks()
+    elif args.lock:
+        run_set_lock(args.lock, locked=True)
+    elif args.unlock:
+        run_set_lock(args.unlock, locked=False)
+    elif args.ticktick_status:
+        config = get_ticktick_config()
+        if not config:
+            logger.error("TickTick not configured. Set TICKTICK_ACCESS_TOKEN in .env")
+            sys.exit(1)
+        show_ticktick_status(config["token"])
+    elif args.weekly_digest:
+        run_weekly_digest(dry_run=args.dry_run)
+    elif args.check_results:
+        run_check_results(
+            target_date=args.date,
+            dry_run=args.dry_run,
+            skip_heartbeat=args.no_heartbeat,
+        )
+    elif args.check_missed_results:
+        _run_safeguard(
+            "EDGAR missed-results backstop",
+            lambda: run_edgar_results_fallback(
+                dry_run=args.dry_run,
+                skip_heartbeat=args.no_heartbeat,
+            ),
+        )
+    elif args.reconcile_calendar:
+        run_reconcile_calendar(dry_run=args.dry_run)
+    elif args.cross_check:
+        _run_safeguard(
+            "cross-check (Finnhub vs yfinance + EDGAR)",
+            lambda: run_cross_check(dry_run=args.dry_run),
+        )
+    elif args.refresh_descriptions:
+        run_refresh_descriptions(dry_run=args.dry_run)
+    elif args.check_announcements:
+        run_check_announcements(dry_run=args.dry_run)
+    elif args.check_ir_emails:
+        run_check_ir_emails(dry_run=args.dry_run)
+    elif args.check_replies:
+        _run_safeguard(
+            "Slack reply processing",
+            lambda: run_check_replies(dry_run=args.dry_run),
+        )
+    elif args.consensus_preview:
+        run_consensus_preview(
+            dry_run=args.dry_run,
+            days_ahead=args.preview_days,
+            ticker=args.preview_ticker,
+        )
+    elif args.cleanup:
+        conn = init_db()
+        cleanup_duplicates(conn, dry_run=args.dry_run)
+        conn.close()
+    else:
+        run(
+            dry_run=args.dry_run,
+            backfill=args.backfill,
+            skip_ticktick=args.no_ticktick,
+            skip_heartbeat=args.no_heartbeat,
+        )
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

     1	"""
     2	Consensus Metrics Preview (StreetAccount Wave 1 §9A).
     3	
     4	Builds a pre-earnings brief for each upcoming covered reporter, composed
     5	entirely from FREE / cached data (yfinance + the SQLite events table +
     6	Coverage Manager exports). One brief per upcoming Tier-1 name carries:
     7	
     8	  - header: company, event date, BMO/AMC badge, last price ± day change
     9	  - mean consensus Rev + EPS (from the DB events table — zero API calls)
    10	  - QTD price move since the prior quarter-end for TICKER / SPY / sector-ETF
    11	  - options-implied move (ATM straddle mid ÷ spot on the first expiry that
    12	    contains the post-earnings reaction — see compute_implied_move)
    13	  - last-4-quarter post-earnings stock reactions
    14	  - EPS beat rate (up to 20 quarters, yfinance Surprise%)
    15	  - conference-call time (from events.call_datetime_utc)
    16	
    17	Two further fields are FMP-Starter-gated (estimate count/low-high range and
    18	the revenue beat rate). They are only fetched when the caller passes an FMP
    19	key AND the kv_store probe flag `fmp_preview_endpoints_ok` == "true"; until
    20	then they render as an explicit "n/a (FMP endpoint unavailable)" — never a
    21	silent blank and never a fabricated number.
    22	
    23	Design invariant: NO field is ever silently dropped. Every degraded field
    24	appends a human note to PreviewRow.na_notes and a machine-readable
    25	{field, reason} entry to PreviewRow.na_fields, and renders as an explicit
    26	"n/a (reason)" string. A per-ticker failure never drops the row.
    27	
    28	This module is additive — it does not touch the daily run() flow.
    29	"""
    30	
    31	from __future__ import annotations
    32	
    33	import io
    34	import logging
    35	import sqlite3
    36	from contextlib import contextmanager, redirect_stderr, redirect_stdout
    37	from dataclasses import dataclass, field
    38	from datetime import date, datetime, timedelta, timezone
    39	from pathlib import Path

    44	except ImportError:  # pragma: no cover - py<3.9 fallback

    56	logger = logging.getLogger("earnings_agent")
    57	
    58	SCHEMA_VERSION = 1
    59	
    60	# Coverage-Manager sector (or subsector) -> sector-proxy ETF for the QTD row.
    61	# Keys are the canonical CM sector labels. Unknown sector -> no ETF row + note.
    62	SECTOR_ETF: dict[str, str] = {
    63	    "Healthcare Services": "XLV",
    64	    "MedTech": "IHI",
    65	    "Large Pharma": "XLV",
    66	    "Biotech": "XBI",
    67	    "Fintech": "XLF",
    68	}
    69	
    70	# Implied-move sanity gates (percent of spot). A straddle mid outside this
    71	# band is almost always a data artifact (stale/one-sided quotes, wrong
    72	# strike), not a real expectation — surface it as n/a rather than a bad number.
    73	_IMPLIED_MOVE_MIN_PCT = 0.5
    74	_IMPLIED_MOVE_MAX_PCT = 40.0
    75	# Nearest common strike must be within this fraction of spot to be "ATM".
    76	_ATM_MAX_STRIKE_DISTANCE = 0.05
    77	# A leg with (ask - bid)/mid above this is flagged "wide market".
    78	_WIDE_MARKET_RATIO = 0.6
    79	# Expiry more than this many days past the reaction date carries extra
    80	# time value; we annotate so the reader knows the move is inflated.
    81	_EXTRA_TIME_VALUE_DAYS = 7
    82	
    83	
    84	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    85	# Dataclasses
    86	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    87	
    88	
    89	@dataclass
    90	class ImpliedMove:
    91	    """Options-implied one-day move from an ATM straddle.
    92	
    93	    pct is None when the move could not be computed for any reason; in that
    94	    case notes[0] carries the "n/a (reason)" string. When pct is present,
    95	    notes holds any annotations ("stale quote", "wide market",
    96	    "(includes N extra days of time value)").
    97	    """
    98	    pct: Optional[float]
    99	    expiry: Optional[str]
   100	    method: str
   101	    notes: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
   102	
   103	    @property
   104	    def ok(self) -> bool:
   105	        return self.pct is not None
   106

   110	    """FMP analyst-estimate spread (count + low/high). All None => n/a."""
   111	    count: Optional[int]
   112	    low: Optional[float]
   113	    high: Optional[float]
   114	
   115	    @property
   116	    def ok(self) -> bool:
   117	        return self.count is not None

   121	class BeatRate:
   122	    """Historical beat rate (beats out of total). beats/total None => n/a."""
   123	    beats: Optional[int]
   124	    total: Optional[int]
   125	    source: str
   126	
   127	    @property
   128	    def ok(self) -> bool:
   129	        return self.total is not None and self.total > 0

   156	class PreviewRow:
   157	    """The fully-assembled preview for one reporter."""
   158	    ticker: str
   159	    company_name: str
   160	    tier: int
   161	    event_date: str
   162	    event_hour: Optional[str]
   163	    call_datetime_utc: Optional[str]
   164	
   165	    last_price: Optional[float] = None
   166	    day_change_pct: Optional[float] = None
   167	
   168	    eps_mean: Optional[float] = None
   169	    rev_mean: Optional[float] = None
   170	    eps_range: EstimateRange = field(

   172	    )
   173	
   174	    qtd_since: Optional[str] = None

   176	    qtd_spx_pct: Optional[float] = None
   177	    sector_etf: Optional[str] = None          # ETF ticker, e.g. "XLV"
   178	    sector_etf_label: Optional[str] = None    # human label, e.g. "Healthcare Services"
   179	    sector_etf_pct: Optional[float] = None
   180	
   181	    implied_move: ImpliedMove = field(
   182	        default_factory=lambda: ImpliedMove(None, None, "ATM straddle", ["n/a (not computed)"])
   183	    )

   186	
   187	    eps_beat: BeatRate = field(default_factory=lambda: BeatRate(None, None, "yfinance"))
   188	    rev_beat: BeatRate = field(default_factory=lambda: BeatRate(None, None, "fmp"))
   189	
   190	    na_notes: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
   191	    na_fields: list[dict] = field(default_factory=list)
   192	
   193	    def mark_na(self, field_name: str, reason: str) -> None:
   194	        """Record a degraded/unavailable field once, both human + machine."""
   195	        self.na_notes.append(f"{field_name}: {reason}")
   196	        self.na_fields.append({"field": field_name, "reason": reason})

   204	@contextmanager
   205	def _silence():
   206	    """Silence yfinance's chatty stdout/stderr (matches market_data idiom)."""
   207	    buf_out, buf_err = io.StringIO(), io.StringIO()
   208	    with redirect_stdout(buf_out), redirect_stderr(buf_err):
   209	        yield

   216	
   217	def _parse_iso_date(s: str) -> Optional[date]:
   218	    try:
   219	        return date.fromisoformat(s[:10])
   220	    except (ValueError, TypeError):
   221	        return None
   222	
   223	
   224	def _prior_quarter_end(today: date) -> date:
   225	    """Return the calendar-quarter-end immediately before `today`'s quarter.
   226	
   227	    For any day in Q3 (Jul-Sep) this is Jun 30; the base for the QTD move.
   228	    """
   229	    q_start_month = ((today.month - 1) // 3) * 3 + 1
   230	    q_start = date(today.year, q_start_month, 1)
   231	    return q_start - timedelta(days=1)
   232	
   233	
   234	def sector_etf_for(sector: str, subsector: str) -> Optional[tuple[str, str]]:
   235	    """Map a CM sector (then subsector) to (label, etf_ticker) or None."""
   236	    for key in (sector, subsector):
   237	        if key and key in SECTOR_ETF:
   238	            return key, SECTOR_ETF[key]
   239	    return None
   240	
   241	
   242	def reaction_date(event_date: str, event_hour: Optional[str]) -> Optional[date]:
   243	    """The trading day whose close reflects the market's reaction.
   244	
   245	    bmo                 -> the event date itself (pre-open release; same-day
   246	                           reaction).
   247	    amc / dmh / blank   -> the next weekday after the event date (post-close
   248	                           or unknown-timing release reacts the following
   249	                           session). Weekend-skip only (no holiday calendar).
   250	    """
   251	    ed = _parse_iso_date(event_date)
   252	    if ed is None:
   253	        return None
   254	    if (event_hour or "").lower() == "bmo":
   255	        return ed
   256	    d = ed + timedelta(days=1)
   257	    while d.weekday() >= 5:  # Sat=5, Sun=6
   258	        d += timedelta(days=1)
   259	    return d
   260

   261	
   262	def _last_close(ticker: str) -> Optional[float]:
   263	    """Most recent daily close from a 5d history (NOT intraday fast_info)."""
   264	    try:
   265	        with _silence():
   266	            hist = yf.Ticker(ticker).history(period="5d", auto_adjust=True)
   267	    except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   268	        logger.debug(f"5d history failed for {ticker}: {exc}")
   269	        return None
   270	    if hist is None or hist.empty:
   271	        return None
   272	    closes = hist["Close"].dropna()
   273	    if closes.empty:
   274	        return None
   275	    return float(closes.iloc[-1])
   276	
   277	
   278	def _leg_mid(row) -> tuple[Optional[float], bool, Optional[float]]:
   279	    """Return (mid, is_stale, spread) for one option leg.
   280	
   281	    Rule (spec §2):
   282	      bid > 0 and ask >= bid  -> (bid + ask) / 2, not stale, spread = ask - bid
   283	      elif lastPrice > 0      -> lastPrice, STALE (no live two-sided quote),
   284	                                 spread unknown (None)
   285	      else                    -> (None, False, None)  -> leg unusable
   286	    """
   287	    def _f(key: str) -> float:
   288	        try:
   289	            v = row.get(key)
   290	        except AttributeError:  # pandas Series
   291	            v = row[key] if key in row else None
   292	        try:
   293	            return float(v) if v is not None else 0.0
   294	        except (TypeError, ValueError):
   295	            return 0.0
   296	
   297	    bid, ask, last = _f("bid"), _f("ask"), _f("lastPrice")
   298	    if bid > 0 and ask >= bid:
   299	        return (bid + ask) / 2.0, False, (ask - bid)
   300	    if last > 0:
   301	        return last, True, None
   302	    return None, False, None
   303	
   304

   306	# Reporter selection

   309	
   310	def _row_to_reporter(raw: tuple, coverage_map: dict[str, TickerInfo]) -> Reporter:
   311	    (ticker, event_date, event_hour, db_tier, company_name,
   312	     eps_est, rev_est, call_dt) = raw
   313	    info = coverage_map.get(ticker)
   314	    return Reporter(
   315	        ticker=ticker,
   316	        company_name=company_name or (info.company_name if info else ""),
   317	        tier=(info.tier if info else (int(db_tier) if db_tier is not None else 99)),
   318	        event_date=event_date,
   319	        event_hour=event_hour,
   320	        call_datetime_utc=call_dt,
   321	        eps_estimate=eps_est,
   322	        rev_estimate=rev_est,
   323	        sector=(info.sector if info else ""),
   324	        subsector=(info.subsector if info else ""),
   325	    )
   326	
   327	
   328	_SELECT_COLS = (
   329	    "ticker, event_date, event_hour, tier, company_name, "
   330	    "eps_estimate, rev_estimate, call_datetime_utc"
   331	)
   332	
   333	
   334	def select_upcoming_reporters(
   335	    conn: sqlite3.Connection,
   336	    coverage: list[TickerInfo],
   337	    *,
   338	    days_ahead: int = 3,
   339	    max_tier: int = 1,
   340	    ticker: Optional[str] = None,
   341	) -> list[Reporter]:
   342	    """Select upcoming, not-yet-reported reporters for previewing.
   343	
   344	    When `ticker` is given, returns that ticker's single nearest upcoming
   345	    unreported event regardless of tier or window (on-demand preview).
   346	    Otherwise returns every unreported event in [today, today+days_ahead]
   347	    whose Coverage-Manager tier is <= max_tier (Tier-1 only by default).
   348	    """
   349	    coverage_map = {t.ticker: t for t in coverage}
   350	    today = date.today()
   351	
   352	    if ticker:
   353	        tk = ticker.strip().upper()
   354	        row = conn.execute(
   355	            f"SELECT {_SELECT_COLS} FROM events "
   356	            "WHERE ticker = ? AND COALESCE(reported, 0) = 0 AND event_date >= ? "
   357	            "ORDER BY event_date LIMIT 1",
   358	            (tk, today.isoformat()),
   359	        ).fetchone()
   360	        if not row:
   361	            logger.warning(f"No upcoming unreported event found for {tk}")
   362	            return []
   363	        return [_row_to_reporter(row, coverage_map)]
   364	
   365	    end = (today + timedelta(days=days_ahead)).isoformat()
   366	    rows = conn.execute(
   367	        f"SELECT {_SELECT_COLS} FROM events "
   368	        "WHERE event_date BETWEEN ? AND ? AND COALESCE(reported, 0) = 0 "
   369	        "ORDER BY event_date, ticker",
   370	        (today.isoformat(), end),
   371	    ).fetchall()
   372	
   373	    reporters: list[Reporter] = []
   374	    for raw in rows:
   375	        rep = _row_to_reporter(raw, coverage_map)
   376	        if rep.tier <= max_tier:
   377	            reporters.append(rep)
   378	    logger.info(
   379	        f"Selected {len(reporters)} upcoming Tier<= {max_tier} reporter(s) "
   380	        f"in next {days_ahead}d ({len(rows)} events scanned)"
   381	    )
   382	    return reporters
   383

   385	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   386	# Free-data field fetchers
   387	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

   389	
   390	def fetch_price_snapshot(ticker: str) -> tuple[Optional[float], Optional[float]]:
   391	    """Return (last_close, 1-day_pct_change) from a single 5d history call."""
   392	    try:
   393	        with _silence():
   394	            hist = yf.Ticker(ticker).history(period="5d", auto_adjust=True)
   395	    except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   396	        logger.debug(f"price snapshot failed for {ticker}: {exc}")
   397	        return None, None
   398	    if hist is None or hist.empty:
   399	        return None, None
   400	    closes = hist["Close"].dropna()
   401	    if closes.empty:
   402	        return None, None
   403	    last = float(closes.iloc[-1])
   404	    if len(closes) >= 2:
   405	        prev = float(closes.iloc[-2])
   406	        day_change = (last - prev) / prev * 100 if prev else None
   407	    else:
   408	        day_change = None
   409	    return last, day_change
   410	
   411	
   412	def fetch_quarter_performance(
   413	    tickers: list[str], since: date
   414	) -> dict[str, Optional[float]]:
   415	    """QTD % change (close on/after `since` -> latest close) for each ticker.
   416	
   417	    One batched yfinance download (the caller pre-adds SPY + sector ETFs so
   418	    the whole panel comes over the wire once). A ticker yfinance can't
   419	    resolve maps to None (caller renders n/a), never raising.
   420	    """
   421	    unique = sorted({t.upper() for t in tickers})
   422	    result: dict[str, Optional[float]] = {t: None for t in unique}
   423	    if not unique:
   424	        return result
   425	
   426	    try:
   427	        with _silence():
   428	            data = yf.download(
   429	                tickers=unique,
   430	                start=since.isoformat(),
   431	                progress=False,
   432	                auto_adjust=True,
   433	                threads=True,
   434	                group_by="ticker",
   435	            )
   436	    except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   437	        logger.warning(f"QTD batch download failed: {exc}")
   438	        return result
   439	
   440	    if data is None or data.empty:
   441	        logger.warning("QTD download returned empty dataset")
   442	        return result
   443	
   444	    for t in unique:
   445	        try:
   446	            if len(unique) == 1:
   447	                closes = data["Close"].dropna()
   448	            else:
   449	                closes = data[t]["Close"].dropna()
   450	            if closes.empty:
   451	                continue
   452	            first = float(closes.iloc[0])
   453	            last = float(closes.iloc[-1])
   454	            if first == 0:
   455	                continue
   456	            result[t] = (last - first) / first * 100
   457	        except (KeyError, IndexError, ValueError) as exc:
   458	            logger.debug(f"QTD unavailable for {t}: {exc}")
   459	    return result
   460	
   461	
   462	def compute_implied_move(
   463	    ticker: str, event_date: str, event_hour: Optional[str]
   464	) -> ImpliedMove:
   465	    """Options-implied move = ATM straddle mid ÷ spot on the first expiry that
   466	    contains the post-earnings reaction date.
   467	
   468	    Never raises and never returns a bad number: every failure mode resolves
   469	    to ImpliedMove(pct=None, ...) whose notes[0] is an explicit "n/a (reason)".
   470	    """
   471	    method = "ATM straddle"
   472	
   473	    rxn = reaction_date(event_date, event_hour)
   474	    if rxn is None:
   475	        return ImpliedMove(None, None, method, ["n/a (unparseable event date)"])
   476	
   477	    try:
   478	        tkr = yf.Ticker(ticker)
   479	        with _silence():
   480	            expiries = list(tkr.options or [])
   481	    except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   482	        return ImpliedMove(
   483	            None, None, method,
   484	            [f"n/a (options unavailable: {exc.__class__.__name__})"],
   485	        )
   486	    if not expiries:
   487	        return ImpliedMove(None, None, method, ["n/a (no listed options)"])
   488	
   489	    future = sorted(
   490	        e for e in expiries
   491	        if (_parse_iso_date(e) is not None and _parse_iso_date(e) >= rxn)
   492	    )
   493	    if not future:
   494	        return ImpliedMove(
   495	            None, None, method,
   496	            ["n/a (no expiry on or after the reaction date)"],
   497	        )
   498	    expiry = future[0]
   499	    exp_date = _parse_iso_date(expiry)
   500	
   501	    spot = _last_close(ticker)
   502	    if spot is None or spot <= 0:
   503	        return ImpliedMove(None, expiry, method, ["n/a (spot price unavailable)"])
   504	
   505	    try:
   506	        with _silence():
   507	            chain = tkr.option_chain(expiry)
   508	        calls, puts = chain.calls, chain.puts
   509	    except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   510	        return ImpliedMove(
   511	            None, expiry, method,
   512	            [f"n/a (option chain fetch failed: {exc.__class__.__name__})"],
   513	        )
   514	
   515	    if calls is None or puts is None or calls.empty or puts.empty:
   516	        return ImpliedMove(None, expiry, method, ["n/a (empty option chain)"])
   517	
   518	    call_strikes = set(calls["strike"].tolist())
   519	    put_strikes = set(puts["strike"].tolist())
   520	    common = call_strikes & put_strikes
   521	    if not common:
   522	        return ImpliedMove(
   523	            None, expiry, method,
   524	            ["n/a (no strike present in both calls and puts)"],
   525	        )
   526	
   527	    K = min(common, key=lambda k: abs(k - spot))
   528	    if abs(K - spot) / spot > _ATM_MAX_STRIKE_DISTANCE:
   529	        return ImpliedMove(
   530	            None, expiry, method,
   531	            [f"n/a (nearest common strike {K:g} is >5% from spot {spot:.2f})"],
   532	        )
   533	
   534	    call_row = calls.loc[calls["strike"] == K].iloc[0]
   535	    put_row = puts.loc[puts["strike"] == K].iloc[0]
   536	    call_mid, call_stale, call_spread = _leg_mid(call_row)
   537	    put_mid, put_stale, put_spread = _leg_mid(put_row)
   538	    if call_mid is None or put_mid is None:
   539	        return ImpliedMove(
   540	            None, expiry, method,
   541	            ["n/a (no usable bid/ask/last on a straddle leg)"],
   542	        )
   543	
   544	    pct = (call_mid + put_mid) / spot * 100
   545	    if not (_IMPLIED_MOVE_MIN_PCT <= pct <= _IMPLIED_MOVE_MAX_PCT):
   546	        return ImpliedMove(
   547	            None, expiry, method,
   548	            [f"n/a (implausible straddle: {pct:.1f}%)"],
   549	        )
   550	
   551	    notes: list[str] = []
   552	    if call_stale or put_stale:
   553	        notes.append("stale quote")
   554	    for spread, mid in ((call_spread, call_mid), (put_spread, put_mid)):
   555	        if spread is not None and mid > 0 and spread / mid > _WIDE_MARKET_RATIO:
   556	            notes.append("wide market")
   557	            break
   558	    if exp_date is not None:
   559	        extra_days = (exp_date - rxn).days
   560	        if extra_days > _EXTRA_TIME_VALUE_DAYS:
   561	            notes.append(f"(includes {extra_days} extra days of time value)")
   562	
   563	    return ImpliedMove(round(pct, 1), expiry, method, notes)
   564	
   565	
   566	def fetch_recent_post_moves(
   567	    conn: sqlite3.Connection, ticker: str, n: int = 4
   568	) -> list[QuarterMove]:
   569	    """Last `n` post-earnings stock reactions, newest first.
   570	
   571	    Prefers the DB's reported events (already timed BMO/AMC), then backfills
   572	    from yfinance's historical earnings dates for names with a thin DB
   573	    history, inferring timing from the timestamp's time-of-day.
   574	    """
   575	    moves: list[QuarterMove] = []
   576	    seen: set[str] = set()
   577	
   578	    rows = conn.execute(
   579	        "SELECT event_date, event_hour FROM events "
   580	        "WHERE ticker = ? AND COALESCE(reported, 0) = 1 AND event_date <= date('now') "
   581	        "ORDER BY event_date DESC LIMIT ?",
   582	        (ticker, n * 3),
   583	    ).fetchall()
   584	    for ev_date, ev_hour in rows:
   585	        if len(moves) >= n:
   586	            break
   587	        if ev_date in seen:
   588	            continue
   589	        mv = fetch_post_earnings_move(ticker, ev_date, ev_hour)
   590	        if mv is not None:
   591	            moves.append(QuarterMove(ev_date, mv.move_pct, mv.window_label))
   592	            seen.add(ev_date)
   593	
   594	    if len(moves) < n:
   595	        try:
   596	            with _silence():
   597	                ed = yf.Ticker(ticker).get_earnings_dates(limit=max(n * 3, 12))
   598	        except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   599	            logger.debug(f"earnings-date backfill failed for {ticker}: {exc}")
   600	            ed = None
   601	        if ed is not None and not ed.empty:
   602	            today = date.today()
   603	            for idx in ed.index:
   604	                if len(moves) >= n:
   605	                    break
   606	                try:
   607	                    d = idx.date()
   608	                except AttributeError:
   609	                    continue
   610	                if d >= today:  # only settled, past reactions
   611	                    continue
   612	                iso = d.isoformat()
   613	                if iso in seen:
   614	                    continue
   615	                try:
   616	                    hour = infer_hour_from_datetime(idx.to_pydatetime())
   617	                except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001
   618	                    hour = None
   619	                mv = fetch_post_earnings_move(ticker, iso, hour)
   620	                if mv is not None:

exec

  1613	
  1614	def run_consensus_preview(
  1615	    dry_run: bool = False,
  1616	    days_ahead: int = 3,
  1617	    ticker: str | None = None,
  1618	):
  1619	    """Build + post the pre-earnings consensus-metrics preview.
  1620	
  1621	    Free/cached data only (yfinance + SQLite + Coverage Manager). The two
  1622	    FMP-Starter B-fields (estimate count/range, revenue beat rate) fire ONLY
  1623	    when FMP_API_KEY is set AND the kv_store probe flag
  1624	    `fmp_preview_endpoints_ok` == "true"; otherwise they render n/a.
  1625	
  1626	    Dedup: kv_store `consensus_preview_posted:TICKER:EVENT_DATE`. Post-then-mark
  1627	    (mark only after a successful Slack post) so a failed post retries.
  1628	    --dry-run writes the JSON export but posts nothing and marks nothing.
  1629	    """
  1630	    import json
  1631	    from pathlib import Path
  1632	
  1633	    coverage = load_coverage()
  1634	    if not coverage:
  1635	        logger.error("No tickers loaded. Cannot build consensus preview.")
  1636	        sys.exit(1)
  1637	    coverage_map = {t.ticker: t for t in coverage}
  1638	
  1639	    conn = init_db()
  1640	
  1641	    reporters = select_upcoming_reporters(
  1642	        conn, coverage, days_ahead=days_ahead, max_tier=1, ticker=ticker
  1643	    )
  1644	
  1645	    # Dedup (live runs only — dry-run must never consult/mutate the ledger,
  1646	    # so a preview is re-previewable on demand).
  1647	    if not dry_run and reporters:
  1648	        pending = []
  1649	        for r in reporters:
  1650	            key = f"consensus_preview_posted:{r.ticker}:{r.event_date}"
  1651	            if kv_get(conn, key):
  1652	                logger.info(
  1653	                    f"Preview already posted for {r.ticker} {r.event_date}; skipping"
  1654	                )
  1655	                continue
  1656	            pending.append(r)
  1657	        reporters = pending
  1658	
  1659	    # FMP gate: both the key AND the probe flag must be present. We never fire
  1660	    # the FMP fetches here otherwise (the probe is run out-of-band).
  1661	    fmp_ok = bool(FMP_API_KEY) and (kv_get(conn, "fmp_preview_endpoints_ok") == "true")
  1662	    logger.info(
  1663	        "FMP preview endpoints gated %s", "ON" if fmp_ok else "OFF (B-fields render n/a)"
  1664	    )
  1665	
  1666	    as_of = date.today()
  1667	    rows = assemble_preview_rows(
  1668	        conn, reporters, coverage_map,
  1669	        fmp_key=(FMP_API_KEY if fmp_ok else None),
  1670	        fmp_ok=fmp_ok,
  1671	    )
  1672	
  1673	    # Window for the export mirrors the selection window (or the single event).
  1674	    if ticker and rows:
  1675	        window = {"start": as_of.isoformat(), "end": rows[0].event_date}
  1676	    else:
  1677	        window = {
  1678	            "start": as_of.isoformat(),
  1679	            "end": (as_of + timedelta(days=days_ahead)).isoformat(),
  1680	        }
  1681	    out_path = Path(__file__).parent / "exports" / "consensus_preview.json"
  1682	    n = write_preview_export(rows, out_path, window)
  1683	    logger.info(f"Wrote {n} consensus preview(s) to {out_path}")
  1684	
  1685	    blocks = build_preview_blocks(rows, as_of)
  1686	    fallback = build_preview_fallback(rows, as_of)
  1687	
  1688	    if dry_run:
  1689	        logger.info("=" * 50)
  1690	        logger.info("DRY RUN — consensus preview fallback text:")
  1691	        logger.info("\n" + fallback)
  1692	        logger.info("-" * 50)
  1693	        logger.info("DRY RUN — Block Kit JSON:")
  1694	        logger.info(json.dumps(blocks, indent=2))
  1695	        logger.info("=" * 50)
  1696	        logger.info("(Dry run — no Slack post, no kv_store marks)")
  1697	        conn.close()
  1698	        return
  1699	
  1700	    if not rows:
  1701	        logger.info("No upcoming reporters to preview — nothing to post.")
  1702	        conn.close()
  1703	        return
  1704	
  1705	    if not SLACK_WEBHOOK_STREET_ACCOUNT:
  1706	        conn.close()
  1707	        raise NotificationError(
  1708	            "SLACK_WEBHOOK_STREET_ACCOUNT not set — cannot post consensus preview"
  1709	        )
  1710	
  1711	    post_slack(SLACK_WEBHOOK_STREET_ACCOUNT, blocks, fallback)
  1712	    # Post-then-mark: only record dedup keys after Slack accepted the message.
  1713	    for r in rows:
  1714	        kv_set(
  1715	            conn,
  1716	            f"consensus_preview_posted:{r.ticker}:{r.event_date}",
  1717	            f"posted:{as_of.isoformat()}",
  1718	        )
  1719	    logger.info(f"Posted consensus preview for {len(rows)} name(s)")
  1720	    conn.close()
  1721	
  1722	
  1723	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1724	# Shared results notification (Slack + TickTick)
  1725	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

  4231	        help="Scan Gmail (via gmail_token.json) for IR-alert emails on Tier 1/2 estimated events; upgrade to confirmed and store the Gmail thread URL",

   620	                if mv is not None:
   621	                    moves.append(QuarterMove(iso, mv.move_pct, mv.window_label))
   622	                    seen.add(iso)
   623	
   624	    moves.sort(key=lambda m: m.event_date, reverse=True)
   625	    return moves[:n]
   626	
   627	
   628	def fetch_eps_beat_history(ticker: str, max_q: int = 20) -> BeatRate:
   629	    """EPS beat rate over up to `max_q` reported quarters (yfinance Surprise%).
   630	
   631	    A positive Surprise(%) is a beat. Rows with NaN surprise (the upcoming,
   632	    not-yet-reported quarter) are excluded. Returns BeatRate with beats/total
   633	    None when yfinance has no usable surprise history (caller renders n/a).
   634	    """
   635	    try:
   636	        with _silence():
   637	            ed = yf.Ticker(ticker).get_earnings_dates(limit=max_q)
   638	    except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   639	        logger.debug(f"EPS beat history failed for {ticker}: {exc}")
   640	        return BeatRate(None, None, "yfinance")
   641	    if ed is None or ed.empty or "Surprise(%)" not in ed.columns:
   642	        return BeatRate(None, None, "yfinance")
   643	    # yfinance does not strictly honor `limit` (it pads future/extra rows), so
   644	    # cap to the most recent max_q reported quarters after dropping the
   645	    # not-yet-reported (NaN-surprise) rows. Index is newest-first.
   646	    surprises = ed["Surprise(%)"].dropna().head(max_q)
   647	    total = int(len(surprises))
   648	    if total == 0:
   649	        return BeatRate(None, None, "yfinance")
   650	    beats = int((surprises > 0).sum())
   651	    return BeatRate(beats, total, "yfinance")
   652	
   653	
   654	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   655	# FMP-gated fetchers (only called when the probe flag is set — see run_*).
   656	# These deliberately never raise; any failure yields an n/a result.
   657	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   658	
   659	
   660	def _fmp_get_json(url: str, timeout: int = 20):
   661	    import json
   662	    import urllib.request
   663	
   664	    with urllib.request.urlopen(url, timeout=timeout) as resp:  # noqa: S310
   665	        return json.load(resp)
   666	
   667	
   668	def fetch_fmp_estimate_range(
   669	    ticker: str, event_date: str, api_key: str
   670	) -> EstimateRange:
   671	    """FMP analyst-estimate spread for the quarter nearest the event date.
   672	
   673	    Endpoint: /api/v3/analyst-estimates/{t}?period=quarter . Gated: only
   674	    invoked when the FMP preview probe has passed. Returns n/a on any error
   675	    or unexpected shape — never a partial/fabricated number.
   676	    """
   677	    if not api_key:
   678	        return EstimateRange(None, None, None)
   679	    url = (
   680	        f"https://financialmodelingprep.com/api/v3/analyst-estimates/"
   681	        f"{ticker}?period=quarter&limit=8&apikey={api_key}"
   682	    )
   683	    try:
   684	        data = _fmp_get_json(url)
   685	    except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   686	        logger.debug(f"FMP estimate-range fetch failed for {ticker}: {exc}")
   687	        return EstimateRange(None, None, None)
   688	    if not isinstance(data, list) or not data:
   689	        return EstimateRange(None, None, None)
   690	
   691	    target = _parse_iso_date(event_date)
   692	
   693	    def _key(row: dict):
   694	        d = _parse_iso_date(str(row.get("date", "")))
   695	        if d is None or target is None:
   696	            return 10 ** 9
   697	        return abs((d - target).days)
   698	
   699	    best = min(data, key=_key)
   700	    count = best.get("numberAnalystEstimatedEps") or best.get("numberAnalystsEstimatedEps")
   701	    low = best.get("estimatedEpsLow")
   702	    high = best.get("estimatedEpsHigh")
   703	    try:
   704	        count = int(count) if count is not None else None
   705	        low = float(low) if low is not None else None
   706	        high = float(high) if high is not None else None
   707	    except (TypeError, ValueError):
   708	        return EstimateRange(None, None, None)
   709	    if count is None or count <= 0:
   710	        return EstimateRange(None, None, None)
   711	    return EstimateRange(count, low, high)
   712	
   713	
   714	def fetch_fmp_rev_beat_history(
   715	    ticker: str, api_key: str, max_q: int = 20
   716	) -> BeatRate:
   717	    """FMP revenue beat rate over up to `max_q` reported quarters.
   718	
   719	    Endpoint: /api/v3/historical/earning_calendar/{t} . Gated like the
   720	    estimate-range fetcher. Returns n/a on any error or unexpected shape.
   721	    """
   722	    if not api_key:
   723	        return BeatRate(None, None, "fmp")
   724	    url = (
   725	        f"https://financialmodelingprep.com/api/v3/historical/earning_calendar/"
   726	        f"{ticker}?limit={max_q}&apikey={api_key}"
   727	    )
   728	    try:
   729	        data = _fmp_get_json(url)
   730	    except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   731	        logger.debug(f"FMP revenue-beat fetch failed for {ticker}: {exc}")
   732	        return BeatRate(None, None, "fmp")
   733	    if not isinstance(data, list) or not data:
   734	        return BeatRate(None, None, "fmp")
   735	
   736	    beats = 0
   737	    total = 0
   738	    for row in data:
   739	        actual = row.get("revenue")
   740	        est = row.get("revenueEstimated")
   741	        if actual is None or est is None:
   742	            continue
   743	        try:
   744	            actual_f, est_f = float(actual), float(est)
   745	        except (TypeError, ValueError):
   746	            continue
   747	        total += 1
   748	        if actual_f > est_f:
   749	            beats += 1
   750	    if total == 0:
   751	        return BeatRate(None, None, "fmp")
   752	    return BeatRate(beats, total, "fmp")
   753	
   754	
   755	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   756	# Row assembly
   757	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   758	
   759	
   760	def assemble_preview_rows(
   761	    conn: sqlite3.Connection,
   762	    reporters: list[Reporter],
   763	    coverage_map: dict[str, TickerInfo],
   764	    *,
   765	    fmp_key: Optional[str] = None,
   766	    fmp_ok: bool = False,
   767	) -> list[PreviewRow]:
   768	    """Assemble one PreviewRow per reporter.
   769	
   770	    QTD is batched across every reporter + SPY + sector ETFs in a single
   771	    yfinance download. Each per-field fetch is wrapped so a single failure
   772	    degrades that field to n/a rather than losing the row; a catastrophic
   773	    per-ticker error still yields a skeleton row flagged in na_fields.
   774	    """
   775	    today = date.today()
   776	    since = _prior_quarter_end(today)
   777	
   778	    # Batch the QTD panel: reporters + SPY + every mapped sector ETF.
   779	    qtd_universe: set[str] = {"SPY"}
   780	    for rep in reporters:
   781	        qtd_universe.add(rep.ticker.upper())
   782	        etf = sector_etf_for(rep.sector, rep.subsector)
   783	        if etf:
   784	            qtd_universe.add(etf[1].upper())
   785	    qtd_map = fetch_quarter_performance(sorted(qtd_universe), since)
   786	
   787	    rows: list[PreviewRow] = []
   788	    for rep in reporters:
   789	        try:
   790	            rows.append(
   791	                _build_row(conn, rep, since, qtd_map, fmp_key=fmp_key, fmp_ok=fmp_ok)
   792	            )
   793	        except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 - never drop a row
   794	            logger.warning(f"Preview assembly failed for {rep.ticker}: {exc}")
   795	            row = PreviewRow(
   796	                ticker=rep.ticker,
   797	                company_name=rep.company_name,
   798	                tier=rep.tier,
   799	                event_date=rep.event_date,
   800	                event_hour=rep.event_hour,
   801	                call_datetime_utc=rep.call_datetime_utc,
   802	                eps_mean=rep.eps_estimate,
   803	                rev_mean=rep.rev_estimate,
   804	            )
   805	            row.mark_na("row", f"assembly failed ({exc.__class__.__name__})")
   806	            rows.append(row)
   807	    return rows
   808	
   809	
   810	def _build_row(
   811	    conn: sqlite3.Connection,
   812	    rep: Reporter,
   813	    since: date,
   814	    qtd_map: dict[str, Optional[float]],
   815	    *,
   816	    fmp_key: Optional[str],
   817	    fmp_ok: bool,
   818	) -> PreviewRow:
   819	    row = PreviewRow(
   820	        ticker=rep.ticker,
   821	        company_name=rep.company_name,
   822	        tier=rep.tier,
   823	        event_date=rep.event_date,
   824	        event_hour=rep.event_hour,
   825	        call_datetime_utc=rep.call_datetime_utc,
   826	        eps_mean=rep.eps_estimate,
   827	        rev_mean=rep.rev_estimate,
   828	        qtd_since=since.isoformat(),
   829	    )
   830	
   831	    if rep.eps_estimate is None:
   832	        row.mark_na("consensus.eps.mean", "no EPS estimate in DB")
   833	    if rep.rev_estimate is None:
   834	        row.mark_na("consensus.revenue.mean", "no revenue estimate in DB")
   835	
   836	    # --- price snapshot ---
   837	    try:
   838	        last, day_change = fetch_price_snapshot(rep.ticker)
   839	    except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   840	        last, day_change = None, None
   841	        logger.debug(f"price snapshot error {rep.ticker}: {exc}")
   842	    row.last_price = last
   843	    row.day_change_pct = day_change
   844	    if last is None:
   845	        row.mark_na("last_price", "yfinance price unavailable")
   846	
   847	    # --- QTD ---
   848	    row.qtd_ticker_pct = qtd_map.get(rep.ticker.upper())
   849	    row.qtd_spx_pct = qtd_map.get("SPY")
   850	    if row.qtd_ticker_pct is None:
   851	        row.mark_na("qtd.ticker_pct", "yfinance QTD unavailable")
   852	    if row.qtd_spx_pct is None:
   853	        row.mark_na("qtd.spx_pct", "yfinance QTD unavailable for SPY")
   854	    etf = sector_etf_for(rep.sector, rep.subsector)
   855	    if etf is None:
   856	        row.mark_na(
   857	            "qtd.sector_etf",
   858	            f"no mapped ETF for sector '{rep.sector or 'unknown'}'",
   859	        )
   860	    else:
   861	        label, etf_ticker = etf
   862	        row.sector_etf = etf_ticker
   863	        row.sector_etf_label = label
   864	        row.sector_etf_pct = qtd_map.get(etf_ticker.upper())
   865	        if row.sector_etf_pct is None:
   866	            row.mark_na("qtd.sector_etf_pct", f"yfinance QTD unavailable for {etf_ticker}")
   867	
   868	    # --- implied move ---
   869	    try:
   870	        row.implied_move = compute_implied_move(
   871	            rep.ticker, rep.event_date, rep.event_hour
   872	        )
   873	    except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 - defensive; compute_* shouldn't raise
   874	        row.implied_move = ImpliedMove(
   875	            None, None, "ATM straddle",
   876	            [f"n/a (unexpected error: {exc.__class__.__name__})"],
   877	        )
   878	    if not row.implied_move.ok:
   879	        reason = row.implied_move.notes[0] if row.implied_move.notes else "n/a"
   880	        row.mark_na("implied_move", reason)
   881	
   882	    # --- post-earnings moves ---
   883	    try:
   884	        row.post_moves = fetch_recent_post_moves(conn, rep.ticker, n=4)
   885	    except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   886	        row.post_moves = []
   887	        logger.debug(f"post-move error {rep.ticker}: {exc}")
   888	    if not row.post_moves:
   889	        row.mark_na("post_earnings_moves", "no computable prior reactions")
   890	
   891	    # --- EPS beat rate ---
   892	    try:
   893	        row.eps_beat = fetch_eps_beat_history(rep.ticker, max_q=20)
   894	    except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   895	        row.eps_beat = BeatRate(None, None, "yfinance")
   896	        logger.debug(f"eps beat error {rep.ticker}: {exc}")
   897	    if not row.eps_beat.ok:
   898	        row.mark_na("beat_rates.eps", "no yfinance surprise history")
   899	
   900	    # --- FMP-gated B-fields ---
   901	    if fmp_ok and fmp_key:
   902	        row.eps_range = fetch_fmp_estimate_range(rep.ticker, rep.event_date, fmp_key)
   903	        if not row.eps_range.ok:
   904	            row.mark_na("consensus.eps.range", "FMP estimate range unavailable")
   905	        row.rev_beat = fetch_fmp_rev_beat_history(rep.ticker, fmp_key, max_q=20)
   906	        if not row.rev_beat.ok:
   907	            row.mark_na("beat_rates.revenue", "FMP revenue-beat history unavailable")
   908	    else:
   909	        row.mark_na("consensus.eps.range", "FMP endpoint unavailable (probe not run)")
   910	        row.mark_na("beat_rates.revenue", "FMP endpoint unavailable (probe not run)")
   911	
   912	    return row
   913	
   914	
   915	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   916	# Rendering helpers
   917	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   918	
   919	
   920	def _fmt_short_date(iso: Optional[str]) -> str:
   921	    d = _parse_iso_date(iso or "")
   922	    if d is None:
   923	        return "n/a"
   924	    return f"{d.strftime('%a %b')} {d.day}"
   925	
   926	
   927	def _fmt_expiry(iso: Optional[str]) -> str:
   928	    d = _parse_iso_date(iso or "")
   929	    if d is None:
   930	        return "n/a"
   931	    return f"{d.strftime('%b')} {d.day}"
   932	
   933	
   934	def _timing_badge(hour: Optional[str]) -> str:
   935	    if not hour:
   936	        return "TBD"
   937	    h = hour.lower()
   938	    return {"bmo": "BMO", "amc": "AMC", "dmh": "DMH"}.get(h, hour.upper())
   939	
   940	
   941	def _fmt_pct(v: Optional[float], *, signed: bool = True, na: str = "n/a") -> str:
   942	    if v is None:
   943	        return na
   944	    if signed:
   945	        return f"{v:+.1f}%"
   946	    return f"{v:.1f}%"
   947	
   948	
   949	def _fmt_price(v: Optional[float]) -> str:
   950	    if v is None:
   951	        return "n/a"
   952	    return f"${v:,.2f}"
   953	
   954	
   955	def _fmt_eps(v: Optional[float]) -> str:
   956	    if v is None:
   957	        return "n/a"
   958	    return f"${v:.2f}"
   959	
   960	
   961	def _fmt_rev(v: Optional[float]) -> str:
   962	    if v is None:
   963	        return "n/a"
   964	    if v >= 1e9:
   965	        return f"${v / 1e9:.2f}B"
   966	    if v >= 1e6:
   967	        return f"${v / 1e6:.1f}M"
   968	    return f"${v:,.0f}"
   969	
   970	
   971	def _fmt_call_et(call_iso: Optional[str], event_date: Optional[str]) -> str:
   972	    """Conference-call time in ET, noting same-day vs next-day."""
   973	    if not call_iso:
   974	        return "n/a"
   975	    try:
   976	        raw = call_iso.replace("Z", "+00:00")
   977	        dt = datetime.fromisoformat(raw)
   978	        if dt.tzinfo is None:
   979	            dt = dt.replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)
   980	    except (ValueError, TypeError):

exec

 succeeded in 0ms:
   980	    except (ValueError, TypeError):
   981	        return "n/a"
   982	    if ZoneInfo is None:
   983	        return dt.strftime("%b %d %H:%M UTC")
   984	    try:
   985	        et = dt.astimezone(ZoneInfo("America/New_York"))
   986	    except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001
   987	        return dt.strftime("%b %d %H:%M UTC")
   988	    hour12 = et.strftime("%I:%M %p").lstrip("0")
   989	    ev = _parse_iso_date(event_date or "")
   990	    if ev is not None and et.date() == ev:
   991	        return f"{hour12} ET (same day)"
   992	    return f"{et.strftime('%a %b')} {et.day} {hour12} ET"
   993	
   994	
   995	def _render_implied_move(im: ImpliedMove) -> str:
   996	    if not im.ok:
   997	        reason = im.notes[0] if im.notes else "n/a"
   998	        return f"Options-implied move: {reason}"
   999	    line = f"Options imply ~{im.pct:.1f}% move ({_fmt_expiry(im.expiry)} exp straddle)"
  1000	    annotations = [n for n in im.notes if n]
  1001	    if annotations:
  1002	        line += " — " + ", ".join(annotations)
  1003	    return line
  1004	
  1005	
  1006	def _render_post_moves(moves: list[QuarterMove]) -> str:
  1007	    if not moves:
  1008	        return "Last post-earnings moves: n/a (no computable prior reactions)"
  1009	    parts = [f"{_fmt_expiry(m.event_date)} {m.move_pct:+.1f}%" for m in moves]
  1010	    return f"Last {len(moves)} post-earnings moves: " + ", ".join(parts)
  1011	
  1012	
  1013	def _render_beat_rate(br: BeatRate, label: str) -> str:
  1014	    if not br.ok:
  1015	        return f"{label}: n/a (FMP endpoint unavailable)" if br.source == "fmp" \
  1016	            else f"{label}: n/a"
  1017	    return f"{label}: {br.beats}/{br.total} ({br.source})"
  1018	
  1019	
  1020	def _render_estimate_range(er: EstimateRange) -> str:
  1021	    if not er.ok:
  1022	        return "est. range n/a (FMP endpoint unavailable)"
  1023	    lo = _fmt_eps(er.low)
  1024	    hi = _fmt_eps(er.high)
  1025	    return f"est. from {er.count} analysts ({lo}-{hi})"
  1026	
  1027	
  1028	def _render_row_lines(row: PreviewRow) -> list[str]:
  1029	    """The full set of spec §-scope lines for one reporter (fallback text)."""
  1030	    badge = _timing_badge(row.event_hour)
  1031	    name = row.company_name or row.ticker
  1032	    day = f" ({_fmt_pct(row.day_change_pct)} day)" if row.day_change_pct is not None else ""
  1033	
  1034	    header = (
  1035	        f"`{row.ticker}` {name} — {_fmt_short_date(row.event_date)} · {badge} · "
  1036	        f"{_fmt_price(row.last_price)}{day}"
  1037	    )
  1038	
  1039	    consensus = (
  1040	        f"Consensus: EPS {_fmt_eps(row.eps_mean)} · Rev {_fmt_rev(row.rev_mean)} · "
  1041	        f"{_render_estimate_range(row.eps_range)}"
  1042	    )
  1043	
  1044	    qtd_bits = [f"{row.ticker} {_fmt_pct(row.qtd_ticker_pct)}",
  1045	                f"S&P 500 (SPY) {_fmt_pct(row.qtd_spx_pct)}"]
  1046	    if row.sector_etf:
  1047	        qtd_bits.append(
  1048	            f"{row.sector_etf_label} ({row.sector_etf}) {_fmt_pct(row.sector_etf_pct)}"
  1049	        )
  1050	    else:
  1051	        qtd_bits.append("sector ETF n/a (no mapped ETF)")
  1052	    qtd = f"QTD since {_fmt_short_date(row.qtd_since)}: " + " · ".join(qtd_bits)
  1053	
  1054	    implied = _render_implied_move(row.implied_move)
  1055	    post = _render_post_moves(row.post_moves)
  1056	    beats = (
  1057	        f"{_render_beat_rate(row.eps_beat, 'EPS beat rate')} · "
  1058	        f"{_render_beat_rate(row.rev_beat, 'Rev beat rate')}"
  1059	    )
  1060	    call = f"Conference call: {_fmt_call_et(row.call_datetime_utc, row.event_date)}"
  1061	
  1062	    return [header, consensus, qtd, implied, post, beats, call]
  1063	
  1064	
  1065	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1066	# Slack builders
  1067	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1068	
  1069	
  1070	SLACK_MAX_BLOCKS = 48
  1071	
  1072	
  1073	def build_preview_fallback(rows: list[PreviewRow], as_of: date) -> str:
  1074	    lines = [
  1075	        f"Consensus previews — {len(rows)} name(s) (as of {_fmt_short_date(as_of.isoformat())})",
  1076	        "",
  1077	    ]
  1078	    if not rows:
  1079	        lines.append("(no upcoming reporters in window)")
  1080	        return "\n".join(lines)
  1081	    for row in rows:
  1082	        lines.extend(_render_row_lines(row))
  1083	        lines.append("")
  1084	    return "\n".join(lines).rstrip()
  1085	
  1086	
  1087	def build_preview_blocks(rows: list[PreviewRow], as_of: date) -> list[dict]:
  1088	    blocks: list[dict] = [
  1089	        {
  1090	            "type": "header",
  1091	            "text": {
  1092	                "type": "plain_text",
  1093	                "text": f"Consensus previews — {len(rows)} name(s)"[:150],
  1094	            },
  1095	        },
  1096	        {
  1097	            "type": "context",
  1098	            "elements": [
  1099	                {
  1100	                    "type": "mrkdwn",
  1101	                    "text": (
  1102	                        f"As of {_fmt_short_date(as_of.isoformat())} · "
  1103	                        "consensus + options-implied moves · free data "
  1104	                        "(yfinance + SQLite)"
  1105	                    ),
  1106	                }
  1107	            ],
  1108	        },
  1109	        {"type": "divider"},
  1110	    ]
  1111	
  1112	    for row in rows:
  1113	        header, *rest = _render_row_lines(row)
  1114	        # header line as its own bold-ish lead, rest as bullet body.
  1115	        body = "\n".join(rest)
  1116	        blocks.append({
  1117	            "type": "section",
  1118	            "text": {"type": "mrkdwn", "text": f"{header}\n{body}"[:2900]},
  1119	        })
  1120	        if row.na_notes:
  1121	            blocks.append({
  1122	                "type": "context",
  1123	                "elements": [
  1124	                    {
  1125	                        "type": "mrkdwn",
  1126	                        "text": "Degraded: " + "; ".join(row.na_notes)[:1900],
  1127	                    }
  1128	                ],
  1129	            })
  1130	
  1131	    if len(blocks) > SLACK_MAX_BLOCKS:
  1132	        blocks = blocks[:SLACK_MAX_BLOCKS]
  1133	    return blocks
  1134	
  1135	
  1136	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1137	# JSON export (mirrors scripts/export_upcoming_events.py contract)
  1138	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1139	
  1140	
  1141	def _beat_rate_json(br: BeatRate) -> dict:
  1142	    return {"beats": br.beats, "total": br.total, "source": br.source}
  1143	
  1144	
  1145	def _row_to_json(row: PreviewRow) -> dict:
  1146	    return {
  1147	        "ticker": row.ticker,
  1148	        "company_name": row.company_name,
  1149	        "tier": row.tier,
  1150	        "event_date": row.event_date,
  1151	        "event_hour": (row.event_hour or "").lower() or None,
  1152	        "call_datetime_utc": row.call_datetime_utc,
  1153	        "last_price": row.last_price,
  1154	        "day_change_pct": row.day_change_pct,
  1155	        "consensus": {
  1156	            "eps": {
  1157	                "mean": row.eps_mean,
  1158	                "count": row.eps_range.count,
  1159	                "low": row.eps_range.low,
  1160	                "high": row.eps_range.high,
  1161	            },
  1162	            "revenue": {
  1163	                "mean": row.rev_mean,
  1164	                "count": None,
  1165	                "low": None,
  1166	                "high": None,
  1167	            },
  1168	        },
  1169	        "qtd": {
  1170	            "since": row.qtd_since,
  1171	            "ticker_pct": row.qtd_ticker_pct,
  1172	            "spx_pct": row.qtd_spx_pct,
  1173	            "sector_etf": row.sector_etf,
  1174	            "sector_etf_pct": row.sector_etf_pct,
  1175	        },
  1176	        "implied_move": {
  1177	            "pct": row.implied_move.pct,
  1178	            "expiry": row.implied_move.expiry,
  1179	            "method": row.implied_move.method,
  1180	            "notes": row.implied_move.notes,
  1181	        },
  1182	        "post_earnings_moves": [
  1183	            {
  1184	                "event_date": m.event_date,
  1185	                "move_pct": m.move_pct,
  1186	                "window_label": m.window_label,
  1187	            }
  1188	            for m in row.post_moves
  1189	        ],
  1190	        "beat_rates": {
  1191	            "eps": _beat_rate_json(row.eps_beat),
  1192	            "revenue": _beat_rate_json(row.rev_beat),
  1193	        },
  1194	        "na_fields": row.na_fields,
  1195	    }
  1196	
  1197	
  1198	def write_preview_export(
  1199	    rows: list[PreviewRow], out_path: Path, window: dict
  1200	) -> int:
  1201	    """Write the versioned preview JSON. Returns the count written.
  1202	
  1203	    Mirrors the upcoming_events.json contract: schema_version, source,
  1204	    generated_at (ISO-Z), window{start,end}, counts{previews}, previews[].
  1205	    """
  1206	    import json
  1207	
  1208	    payload = {
  1209	        "schema_version": SCHEMA_VERSION,
  1210	        "source": "earnings-agent",
  1211	        "generated_at": datetime.now(timezone.utc)
  1212	        .isoformat(timespec="seconds")
  1213	        .replace("+00:00", "Z"),
  1214	        "window": window,
  1215	        "counts": {"previews": len(rows)},
  1216	        "previews": [_row_to_json(r) for r in rows],
  1217	    }
  1218	    out_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
  1219	    out_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
  1220	    return len(rows)

     1	"""
     2	SQLite storage layer — schema management, non-destructive migrations,
     3	and query functions for the earnings events database.
     4	
     5	The database is the source of truth for workflow state and historical memory.
     6	Google Calendar is the source of truth for published event state.
     7	"""
     8	
     9	import sqlite3

    13	from config import DB_PATH

    17	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    18	# Schema version tracking
    19	# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    20	
    21	CURRENT_SCHEMA_VERSION = 12  # Bump when adding migrations
    22	
    23	_MIGRATIONS = {
    24	    # Version 11 → 12: track the earnings conference call timestamp
    25	    # alongside the press-release date. The calendar event itself is
    26	    # anchored to the press release (event_date / event_hour); the call
    27	    # is descriptive context shown in the description. yfinance's
    28	    # earningsCallTimestampStart/End are the primary source. Stored as
    29	    # ISO-8601 with offset (full instant); call_source records which
    30	    # source provided it ('yfinance' for now; 'ir_rss' future).
    31	    12: [
    32	        "ALTER TABLE events ADD COLUMN call_datetime_utc TEXT",
    33	        "ALTER TABLE events ADD COLUMN call_source TEXT",
    34	    ],
    35	
    36	    # Version 10 → 11: yfinance-sourced hour fallback. When Finnhub
    37	    # returns event_hour='' for an upcoming event, we infer 'bmo'/'amc'
    38	    # from yfinance's earnings datetime time-of-day and persist it here.
    39	    # event_hour stays Finnhub-canonical so date_confirmed semantics
    40	    # (notifications.py:765 cross-check verdict) are unchanged. Calendar
    41	    # rendering uses (event_hour or event_hour_yf) for the time block.
    42	    11: [
    43	        "ALTER TABLE events ADD COLUMN event_hour_yf TEXT",
    44	    ],
    45	
    46	    # Version 9 → 10: Track which Slack channel each open-question thread
    47	    # lives in. Cross-check / unseen / reconcile alerts now post to the
    48	    # status-reports channel instead of the earnings channel; the reply
    49	    # poller needs to know which channel to query for each thread. NULL
    50	    # for legacy rows; the poller falls back to SLACK_CHANNEL_ID then.
    51	    10: [
    52	        "ALTER TABLE events ADD COLUMN slack_channel_id TEXT",
    53	    ],
    54	
    55	    # Version 8 → 9: Slack-reply state. Each open question (cross-check
    56	    # disagreement, unseen-ticker, urgent-move) gets its own threaded
    57	    # parent message; replies in that thread drive resolution actions.
    58	    # Also adds a generic kv_store table so things like IR feed URLs can
    59	    # be mutated via Slack reply without committing to the repo.
    60	    9: [

    62	        "ALTER TABLE events ADD COLUMN slack_question_kind TEXT",
    63	        "ALTER TABLE events ADD COLUMN slack_last_reply_ts TEXT",

    75	    # date, when one is detected by the RSS announcement scanner. Stored

    77	    # on events that are already anchored to a specific announcement.
    78	    8: [

    80	    ],
    81	
    82	    # Version 6 → 7: Backfill date_confirmed from event_hour. Every row
    83	    # whose hour is bmo/amc/dmh is retroactively flagged confirmed — the
    84	    # v6 migration only added the column, not the initial values, so
    85	    # rows that don't upsert on the next sync (skip_count path) would
    86	    # otherwise stay at the default 0.
    87	    7: [
    88	        "UPDATE events SET date_confirmed = 1 "
    89	        "WHERE LOWER(COALESCE(event_hour, '')) IN ('bmo', 'amc', 'dmh')",
    90	    ],
    91	
    92	    # Version 5 → 6: Confirmed vs estimated flag. Set to 1 when Finnhub's
    93	    # `hour` field is populated (bmo/amc/dmh) — indicates the company has
    94	    # announced timing, which in practice means the date is confirmed too.
    95	    # Empty hour = Finnhub is projecting from historical cadence; the
    96	    # release date has not been announced by the company.
    97	    6: [
    98	        "ALTER TABLE events ADD COLUMN date_confirmed INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0",
    99	    ],
   100	
   101	    # Version 4 → 5: Record the last yfinance date(s) that the cross-check
   102	    # alerted on for each event. Lets the B1 cross-check suppress daily
   103	    # repeat alerts when the disagreement state hasn't changed, and re-fire
   104	    # when yfinance updates or agreement is restored.
   105	    5: [
   106	        "ALTER TABLE events ADD COLUMN last_xcheck_yf_dates TEXT",
   107	    ],
   108	
   109	    # Version 3 → 4: Human override flag. When date_locked = 1, the sync
   110	    # and reconcile jobs will not move the calendar event's date even if
   111	    # Finnhub disagrees. Used when the user has verified the date via IR
   112	    # and considers Finnhub to be wrong.
   113	    4: [

   115	    ],
   116

   119	    # disappears (possible data loss or coverage drop).
   120	    3: [
   121	        "ALTER TABLE events ADD COLUMN unseen_run_count INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0",
   122	    ],

   181	
   182	def _get_schema_version(conn: sqlite3.Connection) -> int:
   183	    """Get the current schema version from the database."""
   184	    try:
   185	        cur = conn.execute("SELECT version FROM schema_version ORDER BY version DESC LIMIT 1")
   186	        row = cur.fetchone()
   187	        return row[0] if row else 0
   188	    except sqlite3.OperationalError:
   189	        # schema_version table doesn't exist yet
   190	        return 0
   191	
   192	
   193	def _set_schema_version(conn: sqlite3.Connection, version: int):
   194	    """Record the schema version."""
   195	    conn.execute(
   196	        "INSERT INTO schema_version (version, applied_at) VALUES (?, datetime('now'))",
   197	        (version,),
   198	    )
   199	    conn.commit()
   200	
   201	
   202	def _column_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, column: str) -> bool:
   203	    """Check if a column exists in a table."""
   204	    cur = conn.execute(f"PRAGMA table_info({table})")
   205	    return any(row[1] == column for row in cur.fetchall())
   206	
   207	
   208	def _table_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str) -> bool:
   209	    """Check if a table exists."""
   210	    cur = conn.execute(
   211	        "SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name=?",
   212	        (table,),
   213	    )
   214	    return cur.fetchone() is not None
   215	
   216	
   217	def _run_migrations(conn: sqlite3.Connection, current_version: int):
   218	    """Run all pending migrations."""
   219	    for version in sorted(_MIGRATIONS.keys()):
   220	        if version <= current_version:
   221	            continue
   222	
   223	        logger.info(f"Running migration to schema version {version}...")
   224	        for sql in _MIGRATIONS[version]:
   225	            sql_stripped = sql.strip()
   226	            # Skip ALTER TABLE ADD COLUMN if column already exists
   227	            if sql_stripped.upper().startswith("ALTER TABLE") and "ADD COLUMN" in sql_stripped.upper():
   228	                parts = sql_stripped.split()
   229	                # Parse: ALTER TABLE <table> ADD COLUMN <column> ...
   230	                try:
   231	                    table_idx = next(i for i, p in enumerate(parts) if p.upper() == "TABLE") + 1
   232	                    col_idx = next(i for i, p in enumerate(parts) if p.upper() == "COLUMN") + 1
   233	                    table_name = parts[table_idx]
   234	                    col_name = parts[col_idx]
   235	                    if _column_exists(conn, table_name, col_name):
   236	                        logger.debug(f"  Column {table_name}.{col_name} already exists, skipping")
   237	                        continue
   238	                except (StopIteration, IndexError):
   239	                    pass  # Can't parse — just try to run it
   240	
   241	            try:
   242	                conn.execute(sql)
   243	            except sqlite3.OperationalError as e:
   244	                if "duplicate column name" in str(e).lower():
   245	                    logger.debug(f"  Column already exists, skipping: {e}")
   246	                elif "already exists" in str(e).lower():
   247	                    logger.debug(f"  Object already exists, skipping: {e}")
   248	                else:
   249	                    raise
   250	
   251	        _set_schema_version(conn, version)
   252	        logger.info(f"Migration to schema version {version} complete.")
   253	
   254	
   255	def init_db(db_path: Path = DB_PATH) -> sqlite3.Connection:
   256	    """
   257	    Initialize the SQLite database with non-destructive migrations.
   258	
   259	    - Creates the schema from scratch if the database is new.
   260	    - Applies incremental migrations for existing databases.

    10

    12	import json
    13	import logging
    14	from dataclasses import dataclass
    15	from datetime import date, datetime
    16	
    17	try:
    18	    from zoneinfo import ZoneInfo
    19	except ImportError:  # pragma: no cover - py<3.9 fallback
    20	    ZoneInfo = None
    21	
    22	import requests

    24	from digest import DigestData, EventRow
    25	from market_data import PostEarningsMove

    28	@dataclass
    29	class ResultRow:
    30	    ticker: str
    31	    company_name: str
    32	    event_date: str
    33	    event_hour: str | None
    34	    eps_actual: float | None
    35	    eps_estimate: float | None
    36	    rev_actual: float | None
    37	    rev_estimate: float | None
    38	    tier: int
    39	    move: PostEarningsMove | None = None

    41	    subsector: str = ""

    43	    # ISO-8601 datetime (with offset) of the conference call, or None. Drives

    47	logger = logging.getLogger("earnings_agent")
